I wanted to go to Maoyan to check it. But before I reached the door, the door was swiped open with a card from the outside. NS! ! ! Under my exclamation, the visitor did not dare to completely open the door, saying that it was the waiter who came to deliver the fruit. After Fruit was rejected by me, he left.

At that time, I was in a daze, and I was very scared! In my room, my clothes and psychology are very relaxed and safe, but the door of the room was opened directly by the male waiter by swiping his card from the outside! The first reaction at that time was to prevent him from opening my door completely and ask him to leave!

Later, I didn't sleep all night, and the more I thought about it, the more I was afraid, and I felt insecure. Complaint with the front desk at night, and waited for the manager to solve it the next morning. This is obviously a problem of negligence in management and lack of personnel training, but the hotel is explaining that "he has been knocking on the door for a long time, so he opened the door because he thought there was no one inside." May I ask if I can't hear the door knocking in the shower, can he assume that there is no one in the room and can swipe his card to come in? For every room in the hotel, has the guest swiped his card to check in? Can the hotel not see the status?

The manager apologized repeatedly and gave me dinner coupons. In order to stop her apologizing, I accepted it, but any compensation was meaningless to me. I didn't sleep all night and I couldn't think of any reason to calm down.
That's it, Ramada is not short of me as a guest.
